Why are such people being allowed to break the law and order?" ham kab se taliban ban gaye? kya yahi loktantr he? Before Azad Hindustan, Kashmir used to be a separate princely state
 tab kashmir par dogra rajput vansh ke raja hari singh kaa shashan tha
 The Dogra dynasty had earlier conquered Ladakh to unite the entire princely state
 phir 1840 main angrejon se kashmir chhina
 At that time, the borders of this princely state with a population of 40 lakhs were connected to Afghanistan, Russia and China
 isiilie is riyasat kii khaas ahmiyat thi
 After independence in the year 47, then Pakistan was newly formed
 ab ek taraf hindustan tha, duusari taraf pakistan or bich main zamin kaa ye ek chota sa tukdaa kashmir
 An independent state
 or yaheen se shuru hoti he kashmir kii hamaari ye kahani
 70 years ago
 ek qabyli hamalaa hua
 Which ended one year two months one week and three days later
 jisane badal di jananath kii surat
 Which laid the foundation of Jannat to become Jahannam
 jisane pehali baar mujahidin ko paidaa kiya
 Who wrote a new story of Kashmir
 kareeb 700 saal pehle jis gulistaan ko shamsuddin shah mir ne sinchaa tha
 After them all the Nawabs and kings were decorated
 jisaki astaanon or phijaaon main chinar or guldaar kii khushboo tairti thi
 Which later got the title of Jannat of the land
 vahi kashmir
 In the same Kashmir, exactly 70 years ago, the ignorance of a king and the arbitrariness of a hookman made such a poison of ammo in Fijas, which can still be felt in Kashmir today
 meraa mulk
 Your country
 meraa mazahab
 Your religion meri jayeein teri zamin
 My people your people
 is gaiyr insaani zid ne pehle to ek hansate khilakhilaate mulk ke do tukade kar die
 Millions of people were killed in the name of religion and then that paradise was also made as a Jahannam
 jiske raja ne badi ummiido ke saath angrezon se apni riyasat ko hindu-muslim kii siyasat se dur rakhane kii guzarish kii thi
 But the quaid-e-azam Mohammad Ali Jinnah, who created Pakistan for the Muslims sitting near the borders of his princely state, was not ready for this independence of Kashmir
 jinna kii daleel thi ki jis tarah gujarat ke junagarh main hindu avam kii taadaad ko dekhte hue use hindustan main milaayaa gaya, usee tarah kashmir main musalamaanon kii aabaadi ke hisaab se us par sirf or sirf pakistan kaa haq he
 To persuade this stubbornness, Jinnah started pressuring Maharaja Hari Singh of Kashmir
 or kashmir ko jane vaali tamaam zaruri chizon kii supplai band kar di
 Pakistan now used the power to join Kashmir with itself
 magar maharaja hari singh abhi bhi apane us faisle par kaayam the, jo unhone bharat main aakhri waisarai lord mountbeton ko sunaaya tha
 That means free Kashmir
 taarikh- 22 oktober 1947angrezon se mili azaadi ke mahaz 9 hafte baad jinna ke ishaare par pakistan kii taraf se hazaron kabayaliyon ne kashmir main us vaardaat ko anjaam diya
 In which the blood of thousands of innocent Kashmiris was shed
 auraton kii asmat luti gai
 Even the old children were not spared
 lut khasot machaai gai
 The motive was to simply capture Kashmir
 kabayaliyon ke badan par sena kii vardi bhale hi nahin thi
 But there were guns, machine guns and mortars on hand
 saaf tha pakistan ne unhen puri taiyaari ke saath bheja tha
 Jinnah gave him the title of Mujahideen to excite the terrorists
 isi josh main kabayaliyon ne muzaffarabad or domel shahar ke bade hisse par kabza bhi kar liya
 And they reached Uri close to Srinagar
 jinna ek taraf kashmir par hamalaa karvaa rahe the
 On the other hand, their people started provoking Muslim soldiers to create a revolt in the princely state of Kashmir
 kashmir ke jo musalmaan un kabayaliyon ke saath aae wo to mahfuz rahe
 But those who were against, were killed by the terrorists
 mulk kaa nakshaa badalane kii is jang main ghati khun se laal ho gai
 It has been decided that it is impossible for the Maharaja to save Kashmir
 magar isi bich jinna ke bheje bhaade ke aatankiyon ko lut kii lat gai thi
 And he left the mission of Jinnah and went on a mission of plunder
 maharaja hari singh ke saamne ab sirf teen hi raste the
 Let the first thing happen and hand over the princely state of Kashmir to Pakistan
 doosraa un pakistani kabayaliyon se muqabla karen jo narsanhaar par utaaru the
 
 haalanki ye unke liye mumkin nahin lag rahaa tha
 And the third and last way in front of them was to get help from India and save Kashmir
 magar bharat ke saath mushkil ye thi ki tab tak kashmir bharat kaa hissaa nahin tha or aise main bharat sarkaar sainya kaarywai nahin kar sakati thi
